 google ne ise entry level smartfones ke liye pesh kiya tha

 iske liye philippinos main pre orders shuru ho gaye hai

 5,222) in the Philippines
 bharat main isaki keemat bhi isi ke aas paas ho sakati he

 reports ke mutabik bharat Redmi Go pehali timahi se se pehle ho saktaa he
 That is, this smartphone can come to India by March
 haalanki company ne iske bharat launch kii koi bhi baat nahin kari he

 Redmi Go smartphone ke spacifications kii baat karen to isamen 5 inch kii echdi disple di gai he
 It has a Qualcomm Snapdragon 425 processor
 saath hi isamen 1GB ram ke saath 8GB internal memory di gai he
 It can be increased up to 128GB via micro SD card
 Redmi Go main ek rier camera he jo 8 megapixl kaa he
 LED flash has been given with it
 selfi ke liye isamen 5 megapixl kaa front camera diya gaya he
 The battery of this smartphone is 3,000mah
 body plastic kii hogi
 Talking about the software, Android Go has been given in this smartphone
 google ke is android plateform ke saath kai eps bhi hai
 These include apps like Google Go, Files Go, Maps Go, Assistant Go
 edia ye he ki ye eps entry level smartfones ke liye customiod hai
 At the moment it is not clear whether it will have Android Pie or the old Android Oreo
 sarkaar ne ek baar phir se elaan kiya he ki koyale kaa utpaadan badhaane ke apane iraade se vah peeche nahin hati he
 Union Coal Secretary Anil Swarup said at the sixth coal conference to be held in Delhi, "we are surprised by this news published in the newspapers, which says that the government has gone back from the target of 1 billion tonnes of coal production annually
" ham itane utpaadan ke lakshya ke liye patibaddh hai
 " koyala sachiv kaa yah bayaan aise vakt main aayaa he jab desh main bijli kii maang ghati he or hamaare power plants main koyale kii bharpoor supplai he
 The government itself believes that there is currently about 3 weeks of coal supply in all power plants
 "yah sach he ki abhi power demand kam he, lekin jis gati se hamen vikaas dar badhaani he, yah nahin kaha ja saktaa ki power demand kam hi rahegi or koyale kii maang nahin badhegi
 We should prepare it from now
 " koyala sachiv ne patrakaron se kaha ki desh main abhi salanaa koyala utpaadan kareeb 60 karod ton he
 The government wants to increase it to 1 billion tonnes annually by 2020, but environmentally sound institutions and experts are saying this goal of producing coal is worthless
 dilli sthit centre for science and invyrenment yani siesai ke up nideshak chandra bhushan ne enditivi india se kaha, koyala bhavishya nahin he
 In the coming days, the price of non-conventional alternatives to energy will come down and the power from coal will be expensive
 main yah nahin kah rahaa hum ki ham koyale se turant nijaat paa sakate hai
 We cannot get rid of coal even in the next 10 years
 koyale se paidaa hone vaali bijli hamaare base lod kaa kaam karti rahegi lekin pawan urja or saura urja samet gaiyr parmparik stroton se milane vaali urjaakar ko lekar sarkaar ke apane lakshya kaaphi mahatvakankshi he
 If the government wants to generate around 2 lakh MW of electricity from renewable sources by 2022, the goal of producing 1 billion tons of coal does not make any sense
 " The total installed capacity of thermal power plants in the country is 1,86,000 MW
 bijli utpaadan ke sabhi sthapit sanyatron kii kul kshamta 3 lakh megawatt he
 However the power consumption is only 1,50,000 mega watts
 iske baavjood abhi 65,000 megawatt ke thermal plant or lagaaye ja rahe hai
 In addition, about 1,70,000 MW thermal plants are proposed
 koyale ke khilaaf muhim chalaati rahi sanstha greenpis ne koyala sammelan kaa virodh karte hue dilli main press conference kii

 "tippaniyan Questions are also arising from the government's own data
 desh main sabhi sanyantron kii bijli utpaadan kshamta kareeb 3 lakh megawatt he, lekin bijli kii maang isaki aadhi hi he

 yani 50,000 megawatt kii kami

 aane vaale dinon main urja ke gaiyr-paaramparik vikalpon kii keemat ghategi or koyale se milane vaali bijli mahangi hogi

 ham agle 10 saalon main bhi koyale se nijaat nahin paa sakate

 bataa den ki sabase pehle kisi company ke diwalia hone par maamla neshnal company lau tribunel (ensielti) ke paas jaataa he
